#######################################################
#
#	Chancellor has a landed independent acquaintance and it can establish an alliance with player
#
#######################################################

character_event = { 
	id = darkages.72236
	title = EVTNAME1972236
	desc = EVTDESC1972236
	picture = GFX_evt_da_state_diplomacy
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	trigger = {
		is_landed = yes
		has_regent = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = da_temp_chancellor_alliance }
		job_chancellor = { 
			opinion = { who = ROOT value =  1 }
		}
		prisoner = no
		is_incapable = no		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			ai = yes
			is_landed = yes
			opinion = { who = ROOT value = -10 }
			NOT = {
				distance = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 300
				}
			}
			NOT = { is_allied_with = ROOT }
		}
		
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 15 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 18 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 21 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  20 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  40 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  60 } }
		}		
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_temp_chancellor_alliance
			duration = 1825
			hidden = yes
			inherit = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972236
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP105 }
		
		job_chancellor = {
        	opinion = {
        		who = ROOT
        		modifier = opinion_happy
       			years = 1
    		}
		}

		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				is_landed = yes
				opinion = { who = ROOT value = -10 }
				NOT = {
					distance = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 300
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_allied_with = ROOT }				
			}
			
			save_event_target_as = da_new_ally
			
			
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
		
			random_list = {
				1 = {			#Success
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						has_education_diplomacy_trigger = yes
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = grey_eminence
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = gregarious
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = socializer
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						trait = silver_tongue
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = kind
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						trait = honest
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						trait = just
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.6
						trait = trusting
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						diplomacy = 12
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						diplomacy = 15
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						diplomacy = 18
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						diplomacy = 21
					}				

					character_event = { id = darkages.72237	days = 90	random = 90 }
					
				}
				
				1 = {	#Failure
				
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = shy
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 3
						trait = paranoid
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = wary
					}					
					modifier = {
						factor = 2.5
						trait = deceitful
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.3
						trait = cruel
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = wroth
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.4
						trait = arbitrary
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.6
						trait = envious
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						NOT = { diplomacy = 8 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.35
						NOT = { diplomacy = 6 }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						NOT = { diplomacy = 4 }
					}				
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						NOT = { diplomacy = 2 }
					}								

					character_event = { id = darkages.72238	days = 90	random = 90 }			
				
				}
			}
		}

	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB1972236
		
		prestige = 25
		
		job_chancellor = {
        	opinion = {
        		who = ROOT
        		modifier = opinion_disappointed
       			years = 5
    		}
		}
		
	}	

}

###############################################################################
#
#		Chancellor comes with an idea to dramatically improve your spouse's diplomacy, thus increasing significantly the State Diplomacy, too
#
###############################################################################

character_event = { 			
	id = darkages.72239
	title = EVTNAME1972239
	desc = EVTDESC1972239
	picture = GFX_evt_da_state_diplomacy
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	trigger = {
		is_landed = yes
		has_regent = no
		job_chancellor = { 
			opinion = { who = ROOT value =  1 }
		}
		prisoner = no
		is_incapable = no		
		is_married = yes
		
		spouse = {
		
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = da_shinning_at_court }
		}

		NOT = { has_character_modifier = da_temp_chancellor_spouse }

	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 15 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 18 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 21 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  20 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  40 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  60 } }
		}		
	}	
	
	immediate = {
	
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_temp_chancellor_spouse
			duration = 7300
			hidden = yes
			inherit = yes
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972239
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP106 }
		treasury = -50
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_obscured_by_spouse
			duration = -1
		}
		
		spouse = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
        		modifier = opinion_happy
    			years = 5
			}			
		}

		set_character_flag = da_spouse_shinning
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB1972239
		
		prestige = 10
		
		spouse = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
        		modifier = opinion_unhappy
    			years = 5
			}			
		}
		
	}	
	
}



character_event = { 	#SUCCESS
	id = darkages.72240
	title = EVTNAME1972240
	desc = EVTDESC1972240
	picture = GFX_evt_da_state_diplomacy
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	trigger = {
	
		has_character_flag = da_spouse_shinning

	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			spouse = { trait = kind }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.80
			spouse = { trait = charitable }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			spouse = { trait = temperate }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.78
			spouse = { trait = diligent }
		}		
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.65
			spouse = { trait = socializer }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.74
			spouse = { trait = gregarious }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.83
			spouse = { trait = just }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.84
			spouse = { trait = trusting }
		}		

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.91
			spouse = { trait = silver_tongue }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.79
			spouse = { trait = groomed }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.86
			spouse = { trait = proud }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.70
			spouse = { has_education_diplomacy_trigger = yes }
		}		
		
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			4 = {#TOTAL SUCCESS
				modifier = {		#HERE GOES THE SAME MODIFIERS OF THEW PLAYER AS IT DEALS WITH THE MODIFIER AFFECTING HIM
					factor = 1.5
					trait = kind
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = socializer
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					trait = gregarious
				}

				set_character_flag = total_success
				
			}
			4 = {#MAJOR SUCCESS
				modifier = {		#HERE GOES THE SAME MODIFIERS OF THEW PLAYER AS IT DEALS WITH THE MODIFIER AFFECTING HIM
					factor = 1.5
					trait = groomed
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = diligent
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					trait = just
				}

				set_character_flag = major_success
				
			}
			2 = {#MINOR SUCCESS ( INCLUDES TRAITS FROM BOTH SPOUSES)
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					trait = envious
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					trait = cruel
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					trait = wroth
				}				
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.75
					spouse = { trait = envious }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					spouse = { trait = cruel }
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					spouse = { trait = wroth }
				}	

				set_character_flag = minor_success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972240
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = total_success
		}

		prestige = 35
		
		remove_character_modifier = da_obscured_by_spouse

		
		spouse = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_shinning_at_court
				duration = 7300
			}
		}

		clr_character_flag = total_success
		clr_character_flag = da_spouse_shinning
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB1972240
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = major_success
		}

		prestige = 20
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_obscured_by_spouse
			duration = 3650
		}		
		
		
		spouse = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_shinning_at_court
				duration = 3650
			}
		}

		clr_character_flag = major_success
		clr_character_flag = da_spouse_shinning
		
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC1972240
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = minor_success
		}

		prestige = 10
		
		
		spouse = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_shinning_at_court
				duration = 3650
			}
		}

		clr_character_flag = minor_success
		clr_character_flag = da_spouse_shinning
		
	}	
	
	
}

#########################################################################################
#
#	Chancellor contacts a foreign power to lend troops to his liege while at war
#
#########################################################################################

character_event = { 			
	id = darkages.72242
	title = EVTNAME1972242
	desc = EVTDESC1972242
	picture = GFX_evt_da_state_diplomacy
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	trigger = {	
		is_landed = yes
		has_regent = no
		job_chancellor = { 
			opinion = { who = ROOT value =  1 }
		}
		prisoner = no
		is_incapable = no
		war = yes
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = da_temp_chanc_rec_army }
		
		any_independent_ruler = {
			ai = yes
			is_landed = yes
			NOT = {
				distance = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 300
				}
			}
			NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
			NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }			
		}
		
		NOT = { has_earmarked_regiments = da_chancellor_rec_troops }
	
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 180
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 15 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 18 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 21 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  20 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  40 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  60 } }
		}		
	}	
	
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_temp_chanc_rec_army
			duration = 3650
			hidden = yes
			inherit = yes
		}
		
		random_independent_ruler = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				is_landed = yes
				NOT = {
					distance = {
						who = ROOT
						value = 300
					}
				}
				NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
			}
			
			save_event_target_as = da_foreign_leader
			
			
		}		
		
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972242

		event_target:da_foreign_leader = {
			character_event = { id = darkages.72243 days = 15 random = 45 }	#event to pick offer
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB1972242
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP108 }
		
		set_character_flag = da_personal_interference
		
		job_chancellor = {
        	opinion = {
        		who = ROOT
        		modifier = opinion_da_interfered
        		years = 5
        	}			
		}
		
		event_target:da_foreign_leader = {
			character_event = { id = darkages.72243 days = 15 random = 45 }	#event to pick offer
		}
		
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC1972242
		
		prestige = 25
		
	}
	
}

character_event = { 				#Startup event
	id = darkages.72260
	title = EVTNAME1972260
	desc = EVTDESC1972260
	picture = GFX_evt_da_state_diplomacy
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	trigger = {
		is_landed = yes
		has_regent = no
		job_chancellor = { 
			opinion = { who = ROOT value =  1 }
		}
		prisoner = no
		is_incapable = no
		NOT = { has_character_modifier = da_temp_chancellor_diplomatic_overture }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 15 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 18 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { diplomacy = 21 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  20 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  40 } }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			job_chancellor = { opinion = { who = ROOT value =  60 } }
		}		
	}
	
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_temp_chancellor_diplomatic_overture
			days = 7300
			hidden = yes
			inherit = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972260
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP111 }
		treasury = -75

		character_event = { id = darkages.72261 days = 15 random = 85}
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB1972260
		
		
		
	}	
	
}

character_event = { 				#The Geat Hunt - major success
	id = darkages.72284
	title = EVTNAME1972284
	desc = EVTDESC1972284
	picture = GFX_evt_da_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {

	}

	immediate = {
		
		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_character_flag = darkages_a
		}
		
		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_character_flag = darkages_b
		}	

		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_character_flag = darkages_c
		}

		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_character_flag = darkages_d
		}

		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_character_flag = darkages_e
		}	

		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_character_flag = darkages_f
		}

		random = {
			chance = 40
			set_character_flag = darkages_g
		}		

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972284	#Excellent
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP118 }
		
		prestige = 100
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_great_hunt1
			duration = 3650
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = da_extra_risk
			}
			clr_character_flag = da_extra_risk			
			prestige = 100
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = darkages_a
			}
			clr_character_flag = darkages_a
			
			random_voter = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_friend = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }					
				}
				add_friend = ROOT
			}
		}	

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = darkages_b
			}
			clr_character_flag = darkages_b
			
			random_vassal = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }					
				}
				add_friend = ROOT
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = darkages_c
			}
			clr_character_flag = darkages_c
			
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_rival = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_vassal_or_below_of = ROOT }										
					NOT = {
						distance = {
							who = ROOT
							value = 300
						}
					}					
				}
				add_friend = ROOT
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = darkages_d
			}
			clr_character_flag = darkages_d
			
			random_vassal = {
				reverse_add_favor = ROOT
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = darkages_e
			}
			clr_character_flag = darkages_e
			
			random_voter = {
				reverse_add_favor = ROOT
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = darkages_f
			}
			clr_character_flag = darkages_f
			
			random_playable_ruler = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { war_with = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_vassal_or_below_of = ROOT }										
					NOT = {
						distance = {
							who = ROOT
							value = 300
						}
					}					
				}			
				reverse_add_favor = ROOT
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_flag = darkages_g
			}
			clr_character_flag = darkages_g
			
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_caring_ruler
				duration = 7300
			}
		}		

	}

}

	}

			}

						NOT = { trait = robust }
					}
					character_event = { id = darkages.72293 }
				}
				if = {

						has_character_flag = da_training_as_a_heir

					limit = {

				}
				else = {
					character_event = { id = darkages.72290 days = 180 random = 730 }
				}
			}

					days = -1
				}
			}

				limit = {
					NOR = {
						has_province_modifier = stability_2				
						has_province_modifier = stability_1
						has_province_modifier = instability_1
						has_province_modifier = instability_2
					}
				}
				
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = instability_1
					days = -1
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = stability_1
				}
				
				remove_province_modifier = stability_1
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = stability_2
				}

				remove_province_modifier = stability_2
				
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = stability_1
					days = -1
				}
			}

		}

	}


}

#When a previously blackmailed character is not in the council anymore, he/she will not be liable to permanently owe favors to the Liege anymore

character_event = { 		
	id = darkages.72358
	title = EVTNAMEKK1972358
	desc = EVTDESCKK1972358
	picture = GFX_evt_da_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
	
		NOR = { 
			has_job_title = job_spymaster
			has_job_title = job_marshal
			has_job_title = job_chancellor
			has_job_title = job_treasurer
			has_job_title = job_spiritual
		}
		
		has_character_flag = da_blackmailed_by_liege
	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
	
		liege = {
			save_event_target_as = da_liege_blackmailer
		}
	
		clr_character_flag = da_blackmailed_by_liege
		
		remove_opinion = {
			who = event_target:da_liege_blackmailer
			modifier = da_opinion_blackmailed
		}
	}

	
}

character_event = { 		#Maintenance event to control the deletion of personal modifiers given by the religious head
	id = darkages.72384
	title = EVTNAMEKK1972384
	desc = EVTDESC1972384
	picture = GFX_evt_da_easter
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	
	
	trigger = {
		
		ai = no

		OR = {
			has_character_modifier = da_hh_influence
			has_character_modifier = da_hh_praying				
		}
		
		rightful_religious_head_scope = {
			NOT = { has_character_flag = darkages_religious_favour }
		}
		
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
	
	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTAKK1972384
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = da_hh_influence }
			remove_character_modifier = da_hh_influence
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = da_hh_praying }
			remove_character_modifier = da_hh_praying
		}		
		
	}
	
}
